If it was loaded by `require()` before, at this point the instantiation\n   296→    //    is already completed and we can check the whether it is in a cycle\n   297→    //    (in that case the module status is kEvaluaing), and whether the\n   298→    //    required graph is synchronous.\n   299→    // 2. This is only used to create a module graph being require()'d.\n   335→   * @param {string} specifier Specifier of the the imported module.\n   336→   * @param {string} parentURL Where the import comes from.\n   337→   * @param {object} importAttributes import attributes from the import statement.\n   338→   * @returns {ModuleJobBase}\n   339→   */\n   340→  getModuleJobForRequire(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes) {\n   341→    const parsed = URLParse(specifier);\n   342→    if (parsed != null) {\n   343→      const protocol = parsed.protocol;\n   344→      if (protocol === 'https:' || protocol === 'http:') {\n   345→        throw new ERR_NETWORK_IMPORT_DISALLOWED(specifier, parentURL,\n   346→                                                'ES modules cannot be loaded by require() from the network');\n   347→      }\n   348→      assert(protocol === 'file:' || protocol === 'node:' || protocol === 'data:');\n   349→    }\n   350→\n   351→    // TODO(joyeecheung): consolidate cache behavior and use resolveSync() and\n   352→    // loadSync() here.\n   353→    const resolveResult = this.#cachedDefaultResolve(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   354→    const { url, format } = resolveResult;\n   355→    if (!getOptionValue('--experimental-require-module')) {\n   356→      throw new ERR_REQUIRE_ESM(url, true);\n   357→    }\n   358→    const resolvedImportAttributes = resolveResult.importAttributes ?? importAttributes;\n   359→    let job = this.loadCache.get(url, resolvedImportAttributes.type);\n   360→    if (job !== undefined) {\n   361→      // This module is being evaluated, which means it's imported in a previous link\n   362→      // in a cycle.\n   363→      if (job.module.getStatus() === kEvaluating) {\n   364→        const parentFilename = urlToFilename(parentURL);\n   365→        let message = `Cannot import Module ${specifier} in a cycle.`;\n   366→        if (parentFilename) {\n   367→          message += ` (from ${parentFilename})`;\n   368→        }\n   369→        throw new ERR_REQUIRE_CYCLE_MODULE(message);\n   370→      }\n   371→      // Otherwise the module could be imported before but the evaluation may be already\n   372→      // completed (e.g. the require call is lazy) so it's okay. We will return the\n   373→      // module now and check asynchronicity of the entire graph later, after the\n   374→      // graph is instantiated.\n   375→      return job;\n   376→    }\n   377→\n   378→    defaultLoadSync ??= require('internal/modules/esm/load').defaultLoadSync;\n   379→    const loadResult = defaultLoadSync(url, { format, importAttributes });\n   380→\n   381→    // Use the synchronous commonjs translator which can deal with cycles.\n   382→    const finalFormat = loadResult.format === 'commonjs' ? 'commonjs-sync' : loadResult.format;\n   383→\n   384→    if (finalFormat === 'wasm') {\n   385→      assert.fail('WASM is currently unsupported by require(esm)');\n   386→    }\n   387→\n   388→    const { source } = loadResult;\n   389→    const isMain = (parentURL === undefined);\n   390→    const wrap = this.#translate(url, finalFormat, source, isMain);\n   391→    assert(wrap instanceof ModuleWrap, `Translator used for require(${url}) should not be async`);\n   392→\n   393→    if (process.env.WATCH_REPORT_DEPENDENCIES && process.send) {\n   394→      process.send({ 'watch:import': [url] });\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    const cjsModule = wrap[imported_cjs_symbol];\n   398→    if (cjsModule) {\n   399→      assert(finalFormat === 'commonjs-sync');\n   400→      // Check if the ESM initiating import CJS is being required by the same CJS module.\n   401→      if (cjsModule?.[kIsExecuting]) {\n   402→        const parentFilename = urlToFilename(parentURL);\n   403→        let message = `Cannot import CommonJS Module ${specifier} in a cycle.`;\n   404→        if (parentFilename) {\n   405→          message += ` (from ${parentFilename})`;\n   406→        }\n   407→        throw new ERR_REQUIRE_CYCLE_MODULE(message);\n   408→      }\n   409→    }\n   410→\n   411→    const inspectBrk = (isMain && getOptionValue('--inspect-brk'));\n   412→    const { ModuleJobSync } = require('internal/modules/esm/module_job');\n   413→    job = new ModuleJobSync(this, url, importAttributes, wrap, isMain, inspectBrk);\n   414→\n   415→    this.loadCache.set(url, importAttributes.type, job);\n   416→    return job;\n   417→  }\n   418→\n   419→  /**\n   420→   * Translate a loaded module source into a ModuleWrap. This is run synchronously,\n   421→   * but the translator may return the ModuleWrap in a Promise.\n   422→   * @param {string} url URL of the module to be translated.\n   423→   * @param {string} format Format of the module to be translated. This is used to find\n   424→   *                        matching translators.\n   425→   * @param {ModuleSource} source Source of the module to be translated.\n   426→   * @param {boolean} isMain Whether the module to be translated is the entry point.\n   427→   * @returns {ModuleWrap | Promise<ModuleWrap>}\n   428→   */\n   429→  #translate(url, format, source, isMain) {\n   430→    this.validateLoadResult(url, format);\n   431→    const translator = getTranslators().get(format);\n   432→\n   433→    if (!translator) {\n   434→      throw new ERR_UNKNOWN_MODULE_FORMAT(format, url);\n   435→    }\n   436→\n   437→    return FunctionPrototypeCall(translator, this, url, source, isMain);\n   438→  }\n   439→\n   440→  /**\n   441→   * Load a module and translate it into a ModuleWrap for require() in imported CJS.\n   442→   * This is run synchronously, and the translator always return a ModuleWrap synchronously.\n   443→   * @param {string} url URL of the module to be translated.\n   444→   * @param {object} loadContext See {@link load}\n   445→   * @param {boolean} isMain Whether the module to be translated is the entry point.\n   446→   * @returns {ModuleWrap}\n   447→   */\n   448→  loadAndTranslateForRequireInImportedCJS(url, loadContext, isMain) {\n   449→    const { format: formatFromLoad, source } = this.#loadSync(url, loadContext);\n   450→\n   451→    if (formatFromLoad === 'wasm') {  // require(wasm) is not supported.\n   452→      throw new ERR_UNKNOWN_MODULE_FORMAT(formatFromLoad, url);\n   453→    }\n   454→\n   455→    if (formatFromLoad === 'module' || formatFromLoad === 'module-typescript') {\n   456→      if (!getOptionValue('--experimental-require-module')) {\n   457→        throw new ERR_REQUIRE_ESM(url, true);\n   458→      }\n   459→    }\n   460→\n   461→    let finalFormat = formatFromLoad;\n   462→    if (formatFromLoad === 'commonjs') {\n   463→      finalFormat = 'require-commonjs';\n   464→    }\n   465→    if (formatFromLoad === 'commonjs-typescript') {\n   466→      finalFormat = 'require-commonjs-typescript';\n   467→    }\n   468→\n   469→    const wrap = this.#translate(url, finalFormat, source, isMain);\n   470→    assert(wrap instanceof ModuleWrap, `Translator used for require(${url}) should not be async`);\n   471→    return wrap;\n   472→  }\n   473→\n   474→  /**\n   475→   * Load a module and translate it into a ModuleWrap for ordinary imported ESM.\n   476→   * This is run asynchronously.\n   477→   * @param {string} url URL of the module to be translated.\n   478→   * @param {object} loadContext See {@link load}\n   479→   * @param {boolean} isMain Whether the module to be translated is the entry point.\n   480→   * @returns {Promise<ModuleWrap>}\n   481→   */\n   482→  async loadAndTranslate(url, loadContext, isMain) {\n   483→    const { format, source } = await this.load(url, loadContext);\n   484→    return this.#translate(url, format, source, isMain);\n   485→  }\n   486→\n   487→  /**\n   488→   * Load a module and translate it into a ModuleWrap, and create a ModuleJob from it.\n   489→   * This runs synchronously. If isForRequireInImportedCJS is true, the module should be linked\n   490→   * by the time this returns. Otherwise it may still have pending module requests.\n   491→   * @param {string} url The URL that was resolved for this module.\n   492→   * @param {ImportAttributes} importAttributes See {@link getModuleJobForImport}\n   493→   * @param {string} [parentURL] See {@link getModuleJobForImport}\n   494→   * @param {string} [format] The format hint possibly returned by the `resolve` hook\n   495→   * @param {boolean} isForRequireInImportedCJS Whether this module job is created for require()\n   496→   *                                            in imported CJS.\n   497→   * @returns {ModuleJobBase} The (possibly pending) module job\n   498→   */\n   499→  #createModuleJob(url, importAttributes, parentURL, format, isForRequireInImportedCJS) {\n   500→    const context = { format, importAttributes };\n   501→\n   502→    const isMain = parentURL === undefined;\n   503→    let moduleOrModulePromise;\n   504→    if (isForRequireInImportedCJS) {\n   505→      moduleOrModulePromise = this.loadAndTranslateForRequireInImportedCJS(url, context, isMain);\n   506→    } else {\n   507→      moduleOrModulePromise = this.loadAndTranslate(url, context, isMain);\n   508→    }\n   509→\n   510→    const inspectBrk = (\n   511→      isMain &&\n   512→      getOptionValue('--inspect-brk')\n   513→    );\n   514→\n   515→    if (process.env.WATCH_REPORT_DEPENDENCIES && process.send) {\n   516→      process.send({ 'watch:import': [url] });\n   517→    }\n   518→\n   519→    const { ModuleJob } = require('internal/modules/esm/module_job');\n   520→    const job = new ModuleJob(\n   521→      this,\n   522→      url,\n   523→      importAttributes,\n   524→      moduleOrModulePromise,\n   525→      isMain,\n   526→      inspectBrk,\n   527→      isForRequireInImportedCJS,\n   528→    );\n   529→\n   530→    this.loadCache.set(url, importAttributes.type, job);\n   531→\n   532→    return job;\n   533→  }\n   534→\n   535→  /**\n   536→   * This method is usually called indirectly as part of the loading processes.\n   537→   * Use directly with caution.\n   538→   * @param {string} specifier The first parameter of an `import()` expression.\n   539→   * @param {string} parentURL Path of the parent importing the module.\n   540→   * @param {Record<string, string>} importAttributes Validations for the\n   541→   *                                                  module import.\n   542→   * @returns {Promise<ModuleExports>}\n   543→   */\n   544→  async import(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes, isEntryPoint = false) {\n   545→    return onImport.tracePromise(async () => {\n   546→      const moduleJob = await this.getModuleJobForImport(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   547→      const { module } = await moduleJob.run(isEntryPoint);\n   548→      return module.getNamespace();\n   549→    }, {\n   550→      __proto__: null,\n   551→      parentURL,\n   552→      url: specifier,\n   553→    });\n   554→  }\n   555→\n   556→  /**\n   557→   * @see {@link CustomizedModuleLoader.register}\n   558→   */\n   559→  register(specifier, parentURL, data, transferList, isInternal) {\n   560→    if (!this.#customizations) {\n   561→      // `CustomizedModuleLoader` is defined at the bottom of this file and\n   562→      // available well before this line is ever invoked. This is here in\n   563→      // order to preserve the git diff instead of moving the class.\n   564→      // eslint-disable-next-line no-use-before-define\n   565→      this.setCustomizations(new CustomizedModuleLoader());\n   566→    }\n   567→    return this.#customizations.register(`${specifier}`, `${parentURL}`, data, transferList, isInternal);\n   568→  }\n   569→\n   570→  /**\n   571→   * Resolve a module request to a URL identifying the location of the module. Handles customization hooks,\n   572→   * if any.\n   573→   * @param {string|URL} specifier The module request of the module to be resolved. Typically, what's\n   574→   *                               requested by `import specifier`, `import(specifier)` or\n   575→   *                               `import.meta.resolve(specifier)`.\n   576→   * @param {string} [parentURL] The URL of the module where the module request is initiated.\n   577→   *                             It's undefined if it's from the root module.\n   578→   * @param {ImportAttributes} importAttributes Attributes from the import statement or expression.\n   579→   * @returns {Promise<{format: string, url: string}>}\n   580→   */\n   581→  resolve(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes) {\n   582→    specifier = `${specifier}`;\n   583→    if (this.#customizations) {  // Only has module.register hooks.\n   584→      return this.#customizations.resolve(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   585→    }\n   586→    return this.#cachedDefaultResolve(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   587→  }\n   588→\n   589→  /**\n   590→   * Either return a cached resolution, or perform the default resolution which is synchronous, and\n   591→   * cache the result.\n   592→   * @param {string} specifier See {@link resolve}.\n   593→   * @param {string} [parentURL] See {@link resolve}.\n   594→   * @param {ImportAttributes} importAttributes See {@link resolve}.\n   595→   * @returns {{ format: string, url: string }}\n   596→   */\n   597→  #cachedDefaultResolve(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes) {\n   598→    const requestKey = this.#resolveCache.serializeKey(specifier, importAttributes);\n   599→    const cachedResult = this.#resolveCache.get(requestKey, parentURL);\n   600→    if (cachedResult != null) {\n   601→      return cachedResult;\n   602→    }\n   603→    const result = this.defaultResolve(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   604→    this.#resolveCache.set(requestKey, parentURL, result);\n   605→    return result;\n   606→  }\n   607→\n   608→  /**\n   609→   * This is the default resolve step for future synchronous hooks, which incorporates asynchronous hooks\n   610→   * from module.register() which are run in a blocking fashion for it to be synchronous.\n   611→   * @param {string|URL} specifier See {@link resolveSync}.\n   612→   * @param {{ parentURL?: string, importAttributes: ImportAttributes}} context See {@link resolveSync}.\n   613→   * @returns {{ format: string, url: string }}\n   614→   */\n   615→  #resolveAndMaybeBlockOnLoaderThread(specifier, context) {\n   616→    if (this.#customizations) {\n   617→      return this.#customizations.resolveSync(specifier, context.parentURL, context.importAttributes);\n   618→    }\n   619→    return this.#cachedDefaultResolve(specifier, context.parentURL, context.importAttributes);\n   620→  }\n   621→\n   622→  /**\n   623→   * Similar to {@link resolve}, but the results are always synchronously returned. If there are any\n   624→   * asynchronous resolve hooks from module.register(), it will block until the results are returned\n   625→   * from the loader thread for this to be synchornous.\n   626→   * This is here to support `import.meta.resolve()`, `require()` in imported CJS, and\n   627→   * future synchronous hooks.\n   628→   *\n   629→   * TODO(joyeecheung): consolidate the cache behavior and use this in require(esm).\n   630→   * @param {string|URL} specifier See {@link resolve}.\n   631→   * @param {string} [parentURL] See {@link resolve}.\n   632→   * @param {ImportAttributes} [importAttributes] See {@link resolve}.\n   633→   * @returns {{ format: string, url: string }}\n   634→   */\n   635→  resolveSync(specifier, parentURL, importAttributes = { __proto__: null }) {\n   636→    return this.#resolveAndMaybeBlockOnLoaderThread(`${specifier}`, { parentURL, importAttributes });\n   637→  }\n   638→\n   639→  /**\n   640→   * Our `defaultResolve` is synchronous and can be used in both\n   641→   * `resolve` and `resolveSync`. This function is here just to avoid\n   642→   * repeating the same code block twice in those functions.\n   643→   */\n   644→  defaultResolve(originalSpecifier, parentURL, importAttributes) {\n   645→    defaultResolve ??= require('internal/modules/esm/resolve').defaultResolve;\n   646→\n   647→    const context = {\n   648→      __proto__: null,\n   649→      conditions: this.#defaultConditions,\n   650→      importAttributes,\n   651→      parentURL,\n   652→    };\n   653→\n   654→    return defaultResolve(originalSpecifier, context);\n   655→  }\n   656→\n   657→  /**\n   658→   * Provide source that is understood by one of Node's translators. Handles customization hooks,\n   659→   * if any.\n   660→   * @param {string} url The URL of the module to be loaded.\n   661→   * @param {object} context Metadata about the module\n   662→   * @returns {Promise<{ format: ModuleFormat, source: ModuleSource }>}\n   663→   */\n   664→  async load(url, context) {\n   665→    if (this.#customizations) {\n   666→      return this.#customizations.load(url, context);\n   667→    }\n   668→\n   669→    defaultLoad ??= require('internal/modules/esm/load').defaultLoad;\n   670→    return defaultLoad(url, context);\n   671→  }\n   672→\n   673→  /**\n   674→   * This is the default load step for future synchronous hooks, which incorporates asynchronous hooks\n   675→   * from module.register() which are run in a blocking fashion for it to be synchronous.\n   676→   * @param {string} url See {@link load}\n   677→   * @param {object} context See {@link load}\n   678→   * @returns {{ format: ModuleFormat, source: ModuleSource }}\n   679→   */\n   680→  #loadAndMaybeBlockOnLoaderThread(url, context) {\n   681→    if (this.#customizations) {\n   682→      return this.#customizations.loadSync(url, context);\n   683→    }\n   684→    defaultLoadSync ??= require('internal/modules/esm/load').defaultLoadSync;\n   685→    return defaultLoadSync(url, context);\n   686→  }\n   687→\n   688→  /**\n   689→   * Similar to {@link load} but this is always run synchronously. If there are asynchronous hooks\n   690→   * from module.register(), this blocks on the loader thread for it to return synchronously.\n   691→   *\n   692→   * This is here to support `require()` in imported CJS and future synchronous hooks.\n   693→   *\n   694→   * TODO(joyeecheung): consolidate the cache behavior and use this in require(esm).\n   695→   * @param {string} url See {@link load}\n   696→   * @param {object} [context] See {@link load}\n   697→   * @returns {{ format: ModuleFormat, source: ModuleSource }}\n   698→   */\n   699→  #loadSync(url, context) {\n   700→    return this.#loadAndMaybeBlockOnLoaderThread(url, context);\n   701→  }\n   702→\n   703→  validateLoadResult(url, format) {\n   704→    if (format == null) {\n   705→      require('internal/modules/esm/load').throwUnknownModuleFormat(url, format);\n   706→    }\n   707→  }\n   708→\n   709→  importMetaInitialize(meta, context) {\n   710→    if (this.#customizations) {\n   711→      return this.#customizations.importMetaInitialize(meta, context, this);\n   712→    }\n   713→    importMetaInitializer ??= require('internal/modules/esm/initialize_import_meta').initializeImportMeta;\n   714→    meta = importMetaInitializer(meta, context, this);\n   715→    return meta;\n   716→  }\n   717→\n   718→  /**\n   719→   * No-op when no hooks have been supplied.\n   720→   */\n   721→  forceLoadHooks() {\n   722→    this.#customizations?.forceLoadHooks();\n   723→  }\n   724→}\n   725→ObjectSetPrototypeOf(ModuleLoader.prototype, null);\n   726→\n   727→class CustomizedModuleLoader {\n   728→\n   729→  allowImportMetaResolve = true;\n   730→\n   731→  /**\n   732→   * Instantiate a module loader that uses user-provided custom loader hooks.\n   733→   */\n   734→  constructor() {\n   735→    getHooksProxy();\n   736→  }\n   737→\n   738→  /**\n   739→   * Register some loader specifier.\n   740→   * @param {string} originalSpecifier The specified URL path of the loader to\n   741→   *                                   be registered.\n   742→   * @param {string} parentURL The parent URL from where the loader will be\n   743→   *                           registered if using it package name as specifier\n   744→   * @param {any} [data] Arbitrary data to be passed from the custom loader\n   745→   * (user-land) to the worker.\n   746→   * @param {any[]} [transferList] Objects in `data` that are changing ownership\n   747→   * @param {boolean} [isInternal] For internal loaders that should not be publicly exposed.\n   748→   * @returns {{ format: string, url: URL['href'] }}\n   749→   */\n   750→  register(originalSpecifier, parentURL, data, transferList, isInternal) {\n   751→    return hooksProxy.makeSyncRequest('register', transferList, originalSpecifier, parentURL, data, isInternal);\n   752→  }\n   753→\n   754→  /**\n   755→   * Resolve the location of the module.\n   756→   * @param {string} originalSpecifier The specified URL path of the module to\n   757→   *                                   be resolved.\n   758→   * @param {string} [parentURL] The URL path of the module's parent.\n   759→   * @param {ImportAttributes} importAttributes Attributes from the import\n   760→   *                                            statement or expression.\n   761→   * @returns {{ format: string, url: URL['href'] }}\n   762→   */\n   763→  resolve(originalSpecifier, parentURL, importAttributes) {\n   764→    return hooksProxy.makeAsyncRequest('resolve', undefined, originalSpecifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   765→  }\n   766→\n   767→  resolveSync(originalSpecifier, parentURL, importAttributes) {\n   768→    // This happens only as a result of `import.meta.resolve` calls, which must be sync per spec.\n   769→    return hooksProxy.makeSyncRequest('resolve', undefined, originalSpecifier, parentURL, importAttributes);\n   770→  }\n   771→\n   772→  /**\n   773→   * Provide source that is understood by one of Node's translators.\n   774→   * @param {URL['href']} url The URL/path of the module to be loaded\n   775→   * @param {object} [context] Metadata about the module\n   776→   * @returns {Promise<{ format: ModuleFormat, source: ModuleSource }>}\n   777→   */\n   778→  load(url, context) {\n   779→    return hooksProxy.makeAsyncRequest('load', undefined, url, context);\n   780→  }\n   781→  loadSync(url, context) {\n   782→    return hooksProxy.makeSyncRequest('load', undefined, url, context);\n   783→  }\n   784→\n   785→  importMetaInitialize(meta, context, loader) {\n   786→    hooksProxy.importMetaInitialize(meta, context, loader);\n   787→  }\n   788→\n   789→  forceLoadHooks() {\n   790→    hooksProxy.waitForWorker();\n   791→  }\n   792→}\n   793→\n   794→let emittedLoaderFlagWarning = false;\n   795→/**\n   796→ * A loader instance is used as the main entry point for loading ES modules. Currently, this is a singleton; there is\n   797→ * only one used for loading the main module and everything in its dependency graph, though separate instances of this\n   798→ * class might be instantiated as part of bootstrap for other purposes.\n   799→ * @returns {ModuleLoader}\n   800→ */\n   801→function createModuleLoader() {\n   802→  let customizations = null;\n   803→  // Don't spawn a new worker if custom loaders are disabled. For instance, if\n   804→  // we're already in a worker thread created by instantiating\n   805→  // CustomizedModuleLoader; doing so would cause an infinite loop.\n   806→  if (!forceDefaultLoader()) {\n   807→    const userLoaderPaths = getOptionValue('--experimental-loader');\n   808→    if (userLoaderPaths.length > 0) {\n   809→      if (!emittedLoaderFlagWarning) {\n   810→        const readableURIEncode = (string) => ArrayPrototypeReduce(\n   811→          [\n   812→            [/'/g, '%27'], // We need to URL-encode the single quote as it's the delimiter for the --import flag.\n   813→            [/%22/g, '\"'], // We can decode the double quotes to improve readability.\n   814→            [/%2F/ig, '/'], // We can decode the slashes to improve readability.\n   815→          ],\n   816→          (str, { 0: regex, 1: replacement }) => RegExpPrototypeSymbolReplace(hardenRegExp(regex), str, replacement),\n   817→          encodeURIComponent(string));\n   818→        process.emitWarning(\n   819→          '`--experimental-loader` may be removed in the future; instead use `register()`:\\n' +\n   820→          `--import 'data:text/javascript,import { register } from \"node:module\"; import { pathToFileURL } from \"node:url\"; ${ArrayPrototypeJoin(\n   821→            ArrayPrototypeMap(userLoaderPaths, (loader) => `register(${readableURIEncode(JSONStringify(loader))}, pathToFileURL(\"./\"))`),\n   822→            '; ',\n   823→          )};'`,\n   824→          'ExperimentalWarning',\n   825→        );\n   826→        emittedLoaderFlagWarning = true;\n   827→      }\n   828→      customizations = new CustomizedModuleLoader();\n   829→    }\n   830→  }\n   831→\n   832→  return new ModuleLoader(customizations);\n   833→}\n   834→\n   835→\n   836→/**\n   837→ * Get the HooksProxy instance. `lib/internal/modules/run_main.js`, which contains the `shouldUseESMLoader()` function that determines whether the main module should be loaded as ESM based on factors like `--experimental-default-type`, presence of `.mjs` extensions, and custom loaders. This class manages:\\n- Module resolution via the `resolve()` method (which delegates to `defaultResolve()` from resolve.js)\\n- Module loading via the `load()` method (which delegates to `defaultLoad()` from load.js)\\n- Module job creation and caching via `getModuleJobForImport()`\\n- Custom loader hooks support through the `CustomizedModuleLoader` and `HooksProxy` classes\\n\\n## Module Job Pipeline\\nThe `ModuleJob` class in `lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js` manages the loading, linking, instantiation, and evaluation lifecycle:\\n- The `_link()` method resolves all module dependencies\\n- The `instantiate()` method triggers module instantiation via ModuleWrap\\n- The `run()` method evaluates the module\\n\\nA synchronous variant, `ModuleJobSync`, is used for `require()` in imported CJS modules.\\n\\n## Caching\\nThe `ResolveCache` and `LoadCache` classes in `lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js` cache resolution and loading results respectively, maintaining the invariant that identical module requests always resolve to the same result per ECMAScript spec.\\n\\n## ESM Format Translators\\nThe `translators` map in `lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js` contains translator functions for different module formats:\\n- 'module' - WebAssembly modules\\n\\nEach translator converts raw source into a `ModuleWrap` object.\\n\\n## ESM Specifier Resolution\\nThe `lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js` module implements ESM resolution:\\n- `defaultResolve()` - Main resolution function\\n- `packageExportsResolve()` - Resolves package.json exports\\n- `packageImportsResolve()` - Resolves package.json imports\\n- Various resolution helpers for handling package target resolution and conditions\\n\\n## Module Loading\\nThe `lib/internal/modules/esm/load.js` module implements loading:\\n- `defaultLoad()` - Asynchronous loading of module source\\n- `defaultLoadSync()` - Synchronous loading for require() in imported CJS\\n- `getSource()` and `getSourceSync()` - Fetch module source from various protocols\\n\\n## CJS-ESM Interop\\nThe `finalizeEsmResolution()` function in `lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js` bridges CJS and ESM by finalizing ESM resolution results when CJS code loads ESM modules via package.json exports/imports resolution.\\n\\n## Native ModuleWrap C++ Binding\\nThe native `ModuleWrap` class in `src/module_wrap.h` and `src/module_wrap.cc` provides the V8 integration layer:\\n- `ModuleWrap::Link()` - `lib/internal/modules/run_main.js`, which contains the `shouldUseESMLoader()` function that determines whether the main module should be loaded as ESM based on factors like `--experimental-default-type`, presence of `.mjs` extensions, and custom loaders. WebAssembly modules\\n\\nEach translator converts raw source into a `ModuleWrap` object.\\n\\n## ESM Specifier Resolution\\nThe `lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js` module implements ESM resolution:\\n- `defaultResolve()` - Asynchronous loading of module source\\n- `defaultLoadSync()` - Synchronous loading for require() in imported CJS\\n- `getSource()` and `getSourceSync()` - Fetch module source from various protocols\\n\\n## CJS-ESM Interop\\nThe `finalizeEsmResolution()` function in `lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js` bridges CJS and ESM by finalizing ESM resolution results when CJS code loads ESM modules via package.json exports/imports resolution.\\n\\n## Native ModuleWrap C++ Binding\\nThe native `ModuleWrap` class in `src/module_wrap.h` and `src/module_wrap.cc` provides the V8 integration layer:\\n- `ModuleWrap::Link()` -
